26101	Newly renovated! (October 2013 update) Discover the reminiscence of the golden age of Paris when it was known as the capital of the world. That was a time of Universal expositions and great construction projects. The most famous is certainly the Eiffel Tower, but that is not all that remains of the 1889 Universal exposition. The loft we are renting is part of the heritage protected Cite d'artistes building complex which was part of the exhibition around the Efiffel Tower. It was dismantled in the 1920s and rebuild at its present location in the 14th district. Since then the artist's ateliers have been continually used as workshops and living areas. You have an unique opportunity today to admire the ingenious construction from the late of the 19th century and walk in the footsteps of some of the renowned artists of the 20th century. Some of the spaces in the complex still serve as artist's studios.
